**Video**: [Watch](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/080b8674140bd6dd44bf54c1dfb97d43/watch)
![Thumbnail](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/080b8674140bd6dd44bf54c1dfb97d43/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

```
A stylized cinematic 3D animation set on a nighttime city street with wet reflective pavement, soft street lights, and neon glow. An anthropomorphic white rabbit magician stands at the center, wearing a black tailcoat, white shirt, black bow tie, and a black top hat, surrounded by a loose semicircle of onlookers. The rabbit performs smooth, professional card handling with a standard 52-card deck. The deck is fanned evenly at chest height, all cards visible and unique. A hand from the camera selects one card from the fan — the Ace of Hearts. The rabbit takes the same card and holds it clearly facing the camera. The rabbit flicks the card lightly. The Ace of Hearts begins to glow at the edges, then disintegrates into fine red and gold particles. The particles form a controlled, continuous stream with motion trails, flowing forward across the street. The camera follows the particle stream as it travels toward a large glass building facade. Upon impact, a point of light appears and expands outward in a grid-like pattern across the glass surface. The entire building facade activates, and a massive glowing Ace of Hearts forms across it, bright and clearly defined, with subtle pulsing light. After a brief hold, the giant Ace of Hearts breaks apart into particles again. The particles reverse direction, streaming back through the air toward the rabbit. The rabbit steps forward and reaches into the air, catching the incoming particles. In close-up, the particles compress and reform into a single solid playing card in the rabbit’s hand — the Ace of Hearts, unchanged. The rabbit presents the card toward the camera. The camera slowly pulls back, revealing the crowd reacting and clapping, while the city lights and reflections remain vivid in the background.
```

[[Rabbit Magician Street Magic Video]]

### 15. 电影级滑雪视频生成

**Author**: [Gem Alpha](https://x.com/Gemalpha_88)  **Date**: 2026-03-29  **Language**: en

> 这是一份详细的多镜头提示词，用于基于参考图像生成 15 秒的滑雪视频。提示词明确了风格（明亮、清晰、充满运动活力）、电影级运镜语言，以及专注于速度感、利落动作和雪花特效的精确时间轴与镜头设计。

**Video**: [Watch](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/8de6825a35add2595edd059aa901f409/watch)
![Thumbnail](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/8de6825a35add2595edd059aa901f409/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

```
Please generate a skiing video based on the provided reference image. The overall style should be bright, crisp, full of athletic energy, with smooth motion and cinematic camera language. Timeline and shot design as follows:

0–3s: The character from the image smiles at the camera in the snow. Subtle camera shake with snowflakes falling. Background wind noise gradually increases, and a fast-moving flow of wind and snow appears in the frame.

3–5s: Fast cut to an extreme close-up of the character's feet as the ski bindings snap shut, crushing the snow. Simultaneously, the camera rises, transitioning to an overhead view of a steep snowy slope, showing a clear incline as the sense of speed is about to explode.

5–8s: The character slides down from a height at high speed. Shot 1 is a side-front medium follow shot, with the body leaning forward and movements being sharp; Shot 2 cuts to an overhead shot as the steep slope extends downward, with the snow track lines stretching rapidly, creating a strong sense of speed.

8–11s: A series of rapid camera cuts. A low-angle ground shot shows the skis skimming the snow surface as snow powder is kicked up at high speed; a wide shot shows the character making a beautiful turn on the steep slope, their body and the snow line forming a smooth curve.

11–13s: The camera returns to a front-view follow shot as the character charges toward the lens at high speed, performing a sharp turn at close range, sending a massive spray of snow into the air.

13–15s: A large amount of snow powder splashes directly onto the lens, covering the screen in a white snow mist. The camera briefly loses focus before freezing, leaving a strong dynamic afterimage. The overall emphasis is on speed, cutting rhythm, realistic motion, and youthful vitality, with a bright, non-heavy aesthetic that highlights the thrill and freedom of skiing.
```

[[Timestamped Sequence]] [[Sports Cinematography]]

### 16. 第一视角：冰封老鹰救援

Three figures suspended above a shattered coastal megacity under a rotating superstorm:

— a 30-year-old woman wreathed in living lightning, body threaded with branching electric veins, eyes glowing white-hot;

— a towering fire entity formed of molten armor and solar plasma, constantly shedding embers;

— a pale ice sovereign with crystalline skin and flowing frost structures orbiting her form.

Opening frame: medium tri-shot, all three hovering in perfect stillness, storm clouds spiraling around them — the city below already partially flooded and burning.

Hook at second two: all three activate simultaneously.

The storm wielder pulls lightning from the cloud system, the fire entity ignites into full solar output, and the ice sovereign freezes the surrounding atmosphere into expanding crystalline lattices.

The environment fractures into layered systems: lightning chains across buildings, firestorms ignite entire districts, and ice formations suspend debris mid-air.

Each character controls a domain:

— lightning creates branching shock networks across the skyline

— fire generates expanding heat waves and explosive pressure bursts

— ice locks entire sections of the battlefield into geometric suspension

Dynamic orbit camera circles the three-way collision, snap zooming into impact moments where elements clash — lightning striking frozen structures, fire vaporizing ice into explosive steam clouds.

Color logic: white-violet lightning arcs, deep orange fire cores, cobalt ice volumes — each occupying distinct zones of the frame.

Escalation builds as their powers begin interfering — thermal shockwaves fracture frozen structures, lightning supercharges vapor explosions.

Final beat: hard POV shift — camera becomes the collision point itself, plunging downward as all three forces converge into a single detonation wave that obliterates the city center.

Volumetric storm, fire, and ice particle systems interacting in real-time, cinematic destruction physics, 4K ultra-detail.

### 37. 武侠喜剧：猫侠客、鸭书生与哈士奇医生

**Author**: [The Anxious Mind](https://x.com/drjoetw)  **Date**: 2026-03-28  **Language**: zh

> 这是一个为 Seedance 2.0 编写的详细且幽默的提示词，旨在生成一段以深夜中国传统庭院为背景的武侠喜剧视频。剧情讲述了猫侠客审问口含褪黑素胶囊的鸭书生，随后哈士奇医生戏剧性登场干预的故事，画面采用电影级灯光与夸张的动作设计。

**Video**: [Watch](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/de202c2375b54ca5ae34f3e3359f2f1d/watch)
![Thumbnail](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/de202c2375b54ca5ae34f3e3359f2f1d/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

```
影片場景設定 (Global Style)
環境場景：深夜的中式古風庭院，青瓦白牆、紅燈籠隨風微晃，地面有月光與樹影交錯，整體光影帶有濃厚復古武俠電影質感。
角色形象：
橘貓（大俠）：穿著古風俠客服，披風微揚，表情兇狠中帶點憨，氣場十足。
烤鴨（書生）：穿著古代書生長袍，被繩子綁在木樁上，神情委屈又緊張，嘴巴鼓鼓的（含著黑色膠囊）。
哈士奇（醫生）：穿白袍醫生制服，戴黑框眼鏡，神情專業又帶點自信過頭的戲劇感。
道具設定：黑色膠囊（褪黑激素）含在烤鴨嘴中。
畫質要求：電影級打光，超高清 4K，動物毛髮與布料細節清晰，動作流暢，略帶慢動作強化戲劇張力。

分鏡劇情與旁白 (Script & Prompts)

鏡頭 1：武俠審訊（全景/中景）
畫面描述：左側橘貓大俠負手而立，披風隨風微動，右側烤鴨書生被綁在木樁上，嘴巴鼓起。橘貓突然上前，一掌拍在木樁旁，氣勢逼人。
動作：橘貓步步逼近，眼神凌厲。
旁白（橘貓）：
「說！為何不肯交出你嘴中的褪黑激素！」

鏡頭 2：書生鴨死守（烤鴨特寫）
畫面描述：鏡頭推近烤鴨，嘴巴緊閉，臉頰鼓起，眼神倔強又帶點慌張。
動作：烤鴨拼命搖頭，死死咬住膠囊不放。
旁白（烤鴨）：
（含糊不清）「唔唔唔！（我不能給！）」

鏡頭 3：氣氛升溫（橘貓特寫）
畫面描述：橘貓眼神一沉，緩緩抬手，武俠氣場拉滿，背景燈籠微微晃動。
動作：橘貓手指關節發出“喀喀”聲，準備動粗。
旁白（橘貓）：
「敬酒不吃，吃罰酒是吧……」

鏡頭 4：醫生突襲（動作鏡頭）
畫面描述：畫面右側突然衝出哈士奇醫生，一個滑步切入畫面，動作誇張但專業。
動作：哈士奇迅速伸出一掌，「啪！」地按在烤鴨胸口（類似急救按壓）。
音效：低沉“砰”一聲＋誇張彈出音效。

鏡頭 5：膠囊飛出（慢動作特寫）
畫面描述：慢動作鏡頭，烤鴨張嘴，「噗！」一顆黑色膠囊從口中飛出，在空中旋轉。
動作：哈士奇單手優雅接住膠囊，鏡片反光一閃。

鏡頭 6：全場愣住（反應鏡頭）
畫面描述：橘貓與烤鴨同時愣住，畫面定格一瞬，氣氛從緊張瞬間轉為荒謬。
動作：橘貓慢慢轉頭看向哈士奇。
旁白（橘貓，小聲）：
「……這也行？」

鏡頭 7：醫生結尾（哈士奇特寫）
畫面描述：哈士奇推了推眼鏡，手中夾著黑色膠囊，對鏡頭露出自信笑容，背景略微虛化。
動作：微微點頭，語氣專業又帶點得意。
旁白（哈士奇）：
「褪黑激素，不是人人都能吃。」
「最好，先問過醫師。」

鏡頭 8：收尾（全景定格）
畫面描述：三者定格，橘貓仍維持武俠姿勢但表情困惑，烤鴨一臉虛脫，哈士奇自信站中間。背景傳來幾聲夜鳥鳴叫。
動作：畫面定格＋輕微膠片顆粒效果淡出。
```

```
At Sakuragaoka High School, quiet and determined second-year student Haruki Aoyama is publicly humiliated by his nemesis Renji Kurosawa, the intimidating student council vice president, on the very first day of the new semester. What begins as a bitter rivalry fueled by hatred escalates through a high-stakes school competition where both students push each other to the breaking point. As the conflict intensifies, Haruki discovers a shocking truth. Renji's cruelty stems not from malice but from desperate resentment over a scholarship that Haruki unknowingly took, one that Renji's struggling family desperately needed. Forced to confront the gray areas between hero and villain, Haruki must decide whether to destroy his enemy or extend a hand to someone who might just need a friend. The choices he makes will determine whether their rivalry ends in friendship, mutual respect, or lasting regret.

Character:
Haruki Aoyama (Main Protagonist) - A quiet, determined second-year student at Sakuragaoka High School. He is hardworking and principled but struggles with anger and impulsiveness. His journey transforms him from a resentful victim into someone capable of empathy and forgiveness.

Renji Kurosawa (Supporting Character) - The charismatic and ruthless student council vice president who serves as Haruki's nemesis. Beneath his intimidating exterior, he hides deep pain from his family's financial struggles. He is fiercely proud and refuses to show weakness.

Miku Tachibana (Supporting Character) - Haruki's loyal childhood friend and emotional anchor. She is perceptive, strategic, and caring, often serving as the voice of reason. She knows more about the situation than she initially reveals.

Souta Himura (Supporting Character) - A laid-back classmate of Haruki who hides surprising talent beneath his carefree attitude. He becomes a key ally and is unafraid to speak hard truths when needed.

Scene 1:
The Opening 
SalvoIt is the first day of the new semester at Sakuragaoka High School. Haruki Aoyama, a quiet but determined second-year student, arrives hoping for a peaceful school year. However, his nemesis Renji Kurosawa, the charismatic and ruthless student council vice president, publicly humiliates Haruki during the opening assembly by exposing an embarrassing incident from last year. The entire school laughs, and Haruki's reputation is shattered before the year even begins. Haruki's childhood friend Miku Tachibana tries to comfort him, but Haruki is consumed by anger and a desire for payback. The seeds of an intense rivalry are sown as Renji makes it clear he intends to make Haruki's life miserable all year. Storylet: Assembly Confrontation: When Renji takes the stage during the opening ceremony, he publicly targets Haruki with a humiliating story, establishing dominance and triggering Haruki's deep resentment. Hallway Aftermath: After the assembly ends, Haruki retreats to the hallway where Miku finds him; she offers comfort but Haruki is too furious to listen, setting up his emotional state for the chapter. Rival's Warning: Renji corners Haruki near the shoe lockers and delivers a cold warning that this year will be hell for him, escalating the tension and making the conflict personal. Inner Resolve: Alone on the school rooftop after classes, Haruki clenches his fists and silently vows to fight back, establishing his motivation and determination for the story ahead.

Scene 2:
Battle Lines
The school announces a major inter-class competition — the Sakuragaoka Cultural Festival Challenge — where teams compete in academics, sports, and creative arts. Haruki and Renji end up as rival team captains. Haruki rallies his classmates, including the laid-back but surprisingly talented Souta Himura, while Renji uses his influence and intimidation to build an elite squad. As the competition heats up, both rivals push themselves to the limit. Miku serves as Haruki's strategist and emotional anchor. During the sports round, Haruki and Renji face off directly in a relay race that becomes deeply personal. Tensions reach a boiling point when Haruki notices suspicious behavior from Renji's team — possible cheating. The chapter ends at the climax of the competition, with the outcome uncertain. Storylet: Team Formation: When the competition is announced, Haruki must recruit classmates; Souta initially refuses but joins after witnessing Haruki's sincerity, forming the core team. Strategy Session: Miku organizes a late-night study and planning session at Haruki's house, where the team bonds and develops creative strategies, strengthening their resolve. The Relay Showdown: During the sports event, Haruki and Renji run the anchor leg of the relay; the crowd roars as they sprint neck-and-neck, and the raw hatred between them is visible to everyone. Suspicious Evidence: After the academic round, Haruki finds discarded answer sheets near the trash that suggest Renji's team had advance knowledge of the questions, creating a moral dilemma. Miku's Counsel: Miku pulls Haruki aside and warns him that acting on anger alone will make him no different from Renji, forcing him to reflect on his choices.

Scene 3:
Behind the Mask
After the intensity of the competition, a quiet shift begins. Haruki discovers the truth behind Renji's deep-seated hatred — last year, Haruki unknowingly took the scholarship spot that Renji desperately needed to stay in school due to his family's severe financial troubles. Renji's single mother works multiple jobs, and the scholarship was his only hope of easing her burden. The humiliation Renji inflicted on Haruki was born not from cruelty but from desperate resentment. Miku reveals she has known fragments of this story but kept silent to protect both of them. Haruki is shaken, realizing his rival's villain persona is a mask over deep pain. He visits Renji at a part-time job at a convenience store late at night and sees a completely different person — exhausted, vulnerable, and alone. The two share an uncomfortable but honest conversation under the fluorescent lights. Storylet: The Revelation: Miku finally tells Haruki the full story of Renji's family situation after the competition ends, shattering Haruki's simple view of good versus evil. Convenience Store Visit: Haruki tracks down Renji's part-time job and sees him stocking shelves alone late at night, tired and quiet, a stark contrast to his domineering school persona. The Honest Talk: Under harsh convenience store lights, Renji initially lashes out at Haruki for showing up, but eventually breaks down and admits the weight he carries, creating raw emotional vulnerability. Walking Home: The two walk home in silence through empty nighttime streets, neither fully reconciled but with a fragile new understanding forming between them.

Scene 4:
The Price of Exposure
Haruki chose to expose Renji's cheating, and the fallout is catastrophic. The school administration launches a formal investigation, and Renji faces potential expulsion. However, the investigation reveals that Renji was coerced into cheating by a third-year student who wanted to sabotage both teams for his own gain. Renji took the blame silently to protect his teammates. Haruki is horrified — his act of justice may destroy someone who was already a victim. The school is abuzz with gossip and judgment. Souta urges Haruki to fix what he started. Miku is torn between supporting Haruki and feeling that he acted too rashly. Renji, now isolated and facing the disciplinary committee, refuses to defend himself. Haruki must decide whether to step forward and tell the full truth, risking his own standing. Storylet: Investigation Fallout: The school principal announces the investigation results in a tense faculty meeting, and word spreads fast through the student body, turning Renji into a pariah overnight. Souta's Push: Souta confronts Haruki in the empty gym, telling him bluntly that exposing Re

### 39. Boss Battle 场景视频提示词

**Author**: [かし子🍩](https://x.com/Kashiko_AIart)  **Date**: 2026-03-28  **Language**: ja

> 这是一套详细的多部分提示词，旨在生成极具戏剧性的 Boss Battle 场景视频。它指示 AI 仅将参考图用于风格参考，以快速转场作为开端，叠加游戏 UI（RPG 风格指令窗口），并将玩家角色置于前景，面向背景中的大型敌人，整体采用电影级、高对比度的奇幻风格进行渲染。

```
参考画像はリファレンスとしてのみ使用し、スタートフレームには使用しない。バトル風アップテンポBGMあり、効果音あり。開始直後に以下のカットに切り替える。

超高速トランジションで画面切りかえ。高速で空間が崩れ落ちる。

一瞬のホワイトアウトの後、
参考画像の背景の雰囲気を継承したフィールドに切り替わる。

切り替えと同時に、
画面下部にRPG風のコマンドUIが出現する。
そのうちの一つが選択され、キャラクターが動き出す。

UI演出：
・半透明のウィンドウがスライドイン
・ピクセル風またはモダンなゲームUI
・軽く発光する枠（glow）
・カチッとした出現アニメーション

表示内容：
左側：キャラクターの名前、HP、MPゲージ
右側：数種類の参考画像から連想される必殺技(日本語名)
上部：参考画像から連想される敵キャラクター名

参考画像から連想される特殊な巨大な敵キャラクターが右奥に出現し、自キャラは左手前に配置され奥を向いている。

カメラ構図：
・左手前にプレイヤーキャラ
・右奥に敵
・ややローアングルで迫力

演出：
・キャラクターが、その見た目から連想される武器を持ち、戦闘ポーズに入り、敵キャラクターと正対し、軽くステップを踏む。一連の動作は超高速で一瞬で行われる。
・背景は軽く動く（particle, fog, energy）

スタイル：
cinematic, game UI overlay, ultra detailed, high contrast,
fantasy battle scene, dynamic lighting, volumetric light
```

### 43. 童年想象照进现实：赛车视频创作提示

**Author**: [Changning Liu](https://x.com/ChangningL29508)  **Date**: 2026-03-28  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂、多阶段的提示词，详细描述了一个无缝过渡的视频：从一个孩子玩玩具车 (微距写实)，到一个成年人在赛道上驾驶一辆真实的保时捷 911 GT3 (全尺寸力量)。它具体说明了时间安排、摄像机角度 (超低角度跟踪)、灯光、纹理细节，以及一个聚焦于驾驶员眼睛的情感高潮。

**Video**: [Watch](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/d519f538df24987cf95bcb463e6b23c7/watch)
![Thumbnail](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/d519f538df24987cf95bcb463e6b23c7/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

```
0.0 – 4.0 sec — Childhood Imagination (Macro Realism)

Ultra-low-angle macro tracking shot, camera almost touching the ground.
Warm afternoon sunlight spills across a soft beige carpet, visible dust particles floating in air, subtle retro Kodak film warmth (natural, not stylized).

A small child’s hand (only hand visible, no face) pushes a red toy sports car forward.

Camera locks into a front-facing, low tracking perspective, moving with the toy car at increasing speed, mimicking a real race car POV.
Shallow depth of field, realistic motion blur, micro-texture detail on carpet fibers.

Emotion: curiosity → excitement building.

4.0 – 5.5 sec — Transition Through Darkness (Seamless Time Shift)

The toy car speeds into the dark shadow beneath a sofa.

As it enters darkness:

• Light collapses naturally (no artificial fade)
• Carpet texture stretches into subtle motion streaks
• Environment dissolves into full darkness

Seamless transition: the forward motion continues uninterrupted, creating a natural time-space shift (no jump cuts, no glitch effects).

5.5 – 9.0 sec — Reality Emerges (Full-Scale Power)

From darkness, the sound of a real engine ignites.

A real red Porsche 911 GT3 bursts out of shadow into a racetrack environment.

Lighting shifts to sharp, high-contrast daylight.
Cold gray asphalt, heat haze from tires, fine dust particles.

Camera remains low, tracking, and synchronized, maintaining the same motion direction and angle as the toy car shot—creating the illusion it's the same car, now full-scale.

Highly realistic physics:

• Tire grip and vibration
• Subtle suspension movement
• Natural reflections on glossy paint
• Emotion: awe → adrenaline → intensity.

9.0 – 12.0 sec — Human Connection (Emotional Peak)

Cut seamlessly into interior (motion-matched transition).
Close-up: adult driver’s hands gripping a suede racing wheel, wearing professional racing gloves.

Visible micro-details:

• Knuckle tension
• Slight sweat
• Gear shift impact vibration

Camera tilts upward smoothly to reveal the driver’s eyes inside helmet.

Eyes are sharp, focused, intense—mirroring childhood imagination now realized.
Sweat, breath, and subtle helmet reflections visible.

Final moment:
micro freeze-frame feeling (not a hard freeze) on the eyes, with slight camera vibration.
```

[[Seamless Transition]]

```
【镜头1 · 3s · 建立/爆发】 主体一：赛博女性 图片1 ，白色西装，机械颈骨，金齿轮耳环，红唇冷漠，黑发马尾，玄铁长刀 主体二：赛博男性 图片2 ，裸腹六块腹肌，Hello Kitty纹身，黑色机械甲肩臂，粉色金属货裤，白色AJ，武士刀 场景：参考图 图片3 巨型苔藓瀑布崖壁，白色水雾铺天，翠绿蕨类丛生，湿滑苔石 动作：男性从瀑布顶端纵身跃下，武士刀倒握反插，在水雾中高速坠落——子弹时间介入，镜头360度环绕静止身体，水珠悬浮，机械甲齿轮咬合细节锐利可见；时间恢复，男性砸落苔石台炸出十米裂缝，女性横向瞬移闪避，刀锋擦过发丝，黑发寸断飘散 风格：雾山五行国漫画风，硬边水墨线条，青银赤金高对比，电影级光影 镜头：跟随俯冲高速下降，子弹时间360度环绕，相机位于下坠轨迹平行高度(thats where the camera is) 构图：纵向引导线，瀑布与坠落轨迹重合，冲击点为焦点 氛围：极度压迫，生死一线，水雾爆散 音频：风声撕裂；子弹时间静默低频；落地轰鸣；配乐：单鼓重击起 【镜头2 · 4s · 转折/游斗】 主体一：白衣女性，长刀低扫连劈，动作凌厉 主体二：粉裤男性，机械臂格挡，赤金电弧炸裂 场景：瀑布中段苔藓岩壁平台，苔石踩碎，蕨类横飞，水雾被气劲切成丝状 动作：女性贴地滑步突进低扫脚踝——子弹时间介入，极近距特写刀锋与AJ鞋底仅差两毫米，鞋底被刀气削出焦痕，机械关节指节泛白细节定格；时间恢复，男性踏地弹身，燃焰武士刀劈向女性机械颈部，刀锋擦过颈部零件削飞旋转；二人蹬墙互踹，双腿空中碰撞爆发蓝金冲击波，双双震飞后空翻落地 风格：快切与子弹时间交替，打击感极强，细节残酷真实 镜头：贴地低速跟随切极端近距特写，相机位于地面贴近高度(thats where the camera is) 构图：极端近景景深，危险细节锐利，背景瀑布大虚化 氛围：千钧一发，窒息感 音频：刀锋擦骨金属尖啸；鞋底焦痕嗞嗞声；冲击波爆响；配乐：急促弦乐 【镜头3 · 4s · 高潮/环境缠斗】 主体一：白衣女性，长刀反握插地腾空旋踢 主体二：粉裤男性，抓蕨类藤蔓借力甩身，机械臂过载爆红 场景：瀑布底部水潭区，水面踩出巨型凹陷，苔石崩裂，蕨类连根拔起 动作：男性抓整棵蕨类横扫，女性长刀拦腰斩断——子弹时间介入，极近特写断面纤维纹理、刀锋残留绿色汁液、机械关节泛白细节定格；时间恢复，女性借反震旋身斜劈冰蓝刀气，男性机械臂过载硬接握碎，掌心蒸汽焦烟；二人扑摔入水潭缠斗翻滚，激起十米水柱折射金蓝彩虹 风格：慢动作细节特写与暴力冲击并行，环境破坏极致 镜头：子弹时间断面特写切回水柱爆发全景，相机位于水面平行高度(thats where the camera is) 构图：水面倒影与真实动作上下对称，冲击点居中 氛围：野蛮爆裂，生死相搏 音频：树干断裂声；机械过载嗡鸣；水柱爆发轰响；配乐：低频战鼓爆点 【镜头4 · 4s · 终结/大招对轰】 主体一：白衣女性，长刀举顶，银冰光芒过载爆发，西装边缘被能量撕裂 主体二：粉裤男性，武士刀横胸，机械甲赤金全功率过载，粉裤猎猎飞扬 场景：瀑布正前方制高苔石台，百米瀑布为背景，水雾与光芒交融 动作：双方同时蓄力爆发，冰火双色能量柱冲天——子弹时间介入，极近特写女性瞳孔，倒映赤金火焰与男性全影，睫毛水雾微珠清晰，眼神由冷漠转决死；切至男性Hello Kitty纹身特写，纹身在赤金光下线条流动发光；时间恢复，双方全力冲刺对劈，两刀瀑布正中央对撞，炸出五十米冰火双色球形爆炸，瀑布从中间炸裂撕成两半；双方各自倒飞十米重砸苔石，烟尘渐散，二人喘息对望，画面定格 风格：子弹时间微距细节与终极爆炸超广角极致反差，震撼收束 镜头：眼部极端微距切超广角大爆炸全景，相机位于爆炸正面平行高度(thats where the camera is) 构图：爆炸中心点，冰火双色向四方放射，双角色对称分列 氛围：天崩地裂，毁灭级收束 音频：子弹时间静默心跳；双刀碰撞共鸣；爆炸巨响；配乐：单鼓定格，低频余震渐弱 无水印、无字幕、无文字叠加。

[13s–15s] Wide shot of the gym parking lot. He walks toward a toy car, presses a key fob, the headlights flash. He climbs in, revs the engine, and peels out. The car is a hot pink Barbie jeep. He doesn't care.

A tall man in his late 20s with short dark hair and glowing amber eyes, wearing a radiant armor suit of reflective gold plates with molten seams emitting solar energy — opening frame is a medium close-up of him suspended high in the upper atmosphere, clouds far below, sunlight refracting across his armor.

At second two he ignites — the armor flares into full solar output and he descends like a meteor, air igniting around him into plasma trails.

Cloud layers vaporize as he passes through them at extreme velocity.

He maintains rigid posture — both arms slightly extended as energy channels through his body.

The right side emits intense solar flare bursts that incinerate aerial threats; the left generates heat shockwaves that ripple through the atmosphere.

Camera tracks from above, then transitions into a dynamic orbital descent, snap zooming during peak energy bursts and cutting to ground-level impacts.

Color logic: blinding gold-white dominates core frame, fading into deep orange plasma trails.

Suddenly, an explosive aura of blue lightning bursts from his body, crackling and dancing around him. High contrast lighting, sparks of blue energy. Dynamic action shot. Sun Wukong is instantly right in front of the Tiger King. The tiger's eyes widen in fear. Wukong delivers a devastating, full-power body blow with his blue-energy-charged fist directly into the tiger's abdomen. A massive circular shockwave of blue light and energy explodes at the point of impact. Cinematic motion blur. Camera work: Add handheld camera-like movement to enhance the sense of immediacy and tension on the battlefield. For Shot 3, imagine a "speed ramp" effect that accelerates from slow motion. Lighting: High contrast. Use the aura (blue lightning, red fire) itself as the light source (rim light) to sharply outline the character's silhouette. Maximize the contrast with the dark, smoky battlefield to create a mythological atmosphere.
```

### 74. 缝纫大师 - Seedance 2.0 视频提示

**Author**: [Adam也叫吉米](https://x.com/Adam38363368936)  **Date**: 2026-03-27  **Language**: zh

> 这是一个为 Seedance 2.0 设计的、高度详细且包含多个部分的提示，旨在生成一段以“缝纫大师”为主角的电影风格视频。该提示详细说明了主角的外貌、着装、动作风格（融合了咏春拳和太极拳）、环境、氛围，以及一个详细的 15 秒时间线，其中包含具体的摄像机角度和视觉效果，着重强调了精确性、张力以及仪式般的优雅。

**Video**: [Watch](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/d3454d391004027dc80da8f509f24cc7/watch)
![Thumbnail](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/d3454d391004027dc80da8f509f24cc7/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

```
SUBJECTS (主体):
人物： 一位身形极度干练、手臂肌肉线条如钢丝般的女性高定裁缝，眼神冷冽如针尖。
着装： 融合了旗袍元素的深色战术马甲，双臂裸露，前臂缠绕着暗红色的丝绸护腕（用于增加摩擦力）；手指修长且指尖带有金属护具。 
动作风格： 融合了“咏春”的寸劲与“太极”的圆转。动作遵循（蓄力 → 极速出击 → 瞬间静止）的节奏，强调手指的爆发力和丝绸在空中的张力。

ENVIRONMENT (环境):
昏暗的高级私人工作室。背景是整面墙的红木线轴架，成千上万个色块形成几何美感；中心是一张巨大的黑色大理石裁剪台，表面光可鉴人。上方悬挂着单点聚焦的工业冷光灯，空气中漂浮着细微的纤维微粒。

MOOD (氛围):
极度专注、肃杀、带有仪式感的华丽；动作如外科医生般精确，视觉感官上极具压迫性。

TIMELINE (时间线):
0:00-0:02: 特写/广角POV。 裁缝双手撑在黑色大理石台面，低头静止。镜头极速推进，她猛然抬头，双眼锁定镜头（眼神杀）。右手虚空一抓，一匹暗紫色的重磅真丝像长蛇一样从台面滑过，被她单手“锁”住。

0:02-0:05: 剪辑切换/手持感。 裁缝将绸缎抛向空中。她身形如残影，右手持银色长剪，在绸缎下落的瞬间进行“盲剪”。不是普通的裁剪，而是伴随着武术出拳的劲道，剪刀划过空气发出“嗤”的破空声，布料断口极其平整，丝毫不乱。
0:05-0:07: 移动镜头。 她一个侧跨步滑到工作台另一端。单手横扫，数枚钢针从针垫上震起，悬浮在半空。她运劲一推，钢针像暗器一样精准没入远处的衣架样版中，针尾震颤，发出金属鸣音。

0:07-0:10: 连续镜头。 裁缝开始“控线”。她扯出一条金丝，通过手指指缝的缠绕，像操纵傀儡线一样控制绸缎在空中自动折叠、成型。每一次手指的弹拨都伴随着火花般的静电。她用肘部撞击台面，压脚弹起，她瞬间接住并锁死在面料上。

0:10-0:12: 匹配剪辑。 裁缝原地一个急转，外衣下摆如圆阵散开。她双手合拢，将成型的西装领口猛地一拉，最后一道金线在空中划出完美的弧线自动缝合。动作从极快（残影）瞬间切入极慢（定格）。

0:12-0:15: 稳定POV。 尘埃落定。她单手拎起成品礼服，用力一振，礼服在镜头前展开。镜头聚焦在领口的精美刺绣上。她用指甲轻弹纽扣——纽扣颤动。随后她转身走向阴影，留下一道背影，画面被升起的昂贵香水雾气完全覆盖，干净利落地淡出。
```

[[15-Second Timeline]]

```
THE GREAT FISH HEIST — Cat Burglar Kitchen Raid A chubby orange tabby cat with enormous green eyes, wearing a tiny black turtleneck and a miniature ski mask pushed up on his forehead, sneaks across a moonlit kitchen counter toward an unguarded salmon fillet on a cutting board. High budget 3D animation, Pixar quality lighting and fur rendering. [0s–1.5s] Wide shot of a beautiful modern kitchen at night. Moonlight streams through the window. Everything is still. Then two glowing green eyes appear from behind a fruit bowl. [1.5s–3s] The cat rolls across the counter like a secret agent, knocking over a salt shaker. He freezes. Catches it midair with one paw. Places it back. Wipes his brow with immense relief. [3s–5s] He reaches the salmon. His pupils dilate to full circles. A single tear of joy rolls down his cheek. His tail goes rigid like an exclamation mark. He grabs the salmon and stuffs the entire thing in his mouth, cheeks bulging impossibly. [7s–9s] A massive golden retriever slides into the kitchen, paws scrambling on tile, crashing into the refrigerator. The cat is already on top of the fridge, salmon hanging out of his mouth, looking down with pure contempt. [9s–11s] The dog stacks kitchen chairs to reach the fridge. The cat watches, unimpressed, casually chewing. The chair tower wobbles. The dog's eyes go wide. [11s–13s] The chairs collapse. The dog crashes through a tower of pots and pans. An explosion of kitchenware. A colander lands on the dog's head like a helmet. He sits in the wreckage, tail still wagging. [13s–15s] The cat drops the fish skeleton on the dog's head, pulls down his ski mask, and moonwalks across the counter toward the window. He turns back, salutes, and disappears into the night. Cut to black. 3D animated, Pixar quality fur and lighting, kitchen heist, cat vs dog comedy, moonlit slapstick, cinematic, 4K.

原创赛博武侠动作巨制(Original Cyber Wuxia Action Epic)。8K电影级画质，高帧率摄影。 核心风格：超高速机械武术(Hyper-speed Mechanical Martial Arts)。强调“宗师级的见招拆招”、“残影移动”和“极致的物理碰撞”。 安全与版权优化（关键）： 1. 角色完全原创：通用型设计，避开任何知名IP特征。 2. 激烈感来源：通过极快的剪辑节奏、漫天的焊接火花(Welding Sparks)、高压蒸汽喷射(High-pressure Steam)和地面震荡来体现，不出现肢解。 3. 分镜策略：采用好莱坞动作片式的多机位快速切换。 【场景】 被暴雨笼罩的赛博朋克古塔废墟顶部(Cyberpunk Pagoda Ruins Rooftop)。电闪雷鸣，地面是积水的青石板和霓虹灯倒影。 【角色设计（原创宗师机甲）】 1. “疾风刃”(Gale Blade)：敏捷型。修长、哑光黑与银色相间，背负一把发光的**等离子唐刀(Plasma Katana)**。风格：快准狠的剑客。 2. “不动尊”(Iron Fortress)：力量型。魁梧、重型古铜色装甲，双臂装备有**液压冲击拳套(Hydraulic Impact Gauntlets)**。风格：硬气功与重拳。 【分镜脚本 (约25秒高燃剪辑)】 [00:00-00:04] 镜头1：雨中对峙·气机锁定 机位：极稳的中景接特写(Stable Mid-shot to Macro Close-up)。 动作：暴雨倾盆。两台机甲静止对立。 细节特写：雨水打在“不动尊”炽热的肩甲上瞬间蒸发成白雾。镜头快速推向“疾风刃”的光学眼睛，光圈急剧收缩锁定目标。引擎启动的低频轰鸣声。 [00:04-00:08] 镜头2：瞬动·第一回合爆裂 机位：侧面极速跟随接快速剪辑(Side High-speed Tracking into Rapid Cuts)。 动作：“疾风刃”瞬间消失，拉出一道残影冲锋。“不动尊”重拳迎击。 激烈对撞：两台机甲在0.1秒内发生了十几次高频肢体碰撞。每一次格挡都爆出**瀑布般耀眼的金色电焊火花(Cascading Welding Sparks)**，照亮了黑暗的雨夜。 [00:08-00:12] 镜头3：凌空机动·踏浪而行 机位：低角度广角仰拍(Low-angle Wide Shot)。 动作：“疾风刃”利用反作用力腾空而起，双脚在废墟的墙面上飞速奔跑（飞檐走壁），脚下踩碎瓦片，激起一串水龙。 [00:12-00:16] 镜头4：重拳轰炸·环境破坏 机位：主观视角接冲击特写(POV into Impact Close-up)。 动作：“不动尊”预判了空中的轨迹，一记蓄力重拳轰在墙面上。 视觉奇观：整面赛博古墙在巨大的机械力量下**轰然炸裂(Explosive坍塌)**，无数砖石和钢筋碎片像炮弹一样四处飞溅。 [00:16-00:20] 镜头5：拔刀·光影剑舞 机位：环绕慢动作(Orbit Slow-mo)。 动作：“疾风刃”在坠落中拔出背后的**等离子唐刀**，刀身发出刺眼的蓝白光芒。它在空中完成了一个华丽的旋风斩。 特效：雨水被高温刀锋瞬间汽化，形成一圈白色的蒸汽圆环。 [00:20-00:25] 镜头6：终极碰撞·寸劲开天 机位：超广角定格接冲击波震荡(Ultra-wide Freeze Frame to Shockwave Shake)。 动作：“不动尊”双臂交叉格挡，“疾风刃”的等离子刀狠狠斩在上面。 结局：能量武器与重型装甲的终极对撞。 特效：以接触点为中心，爆发出一团巨大的**球形能量冲击波(Massive Energy Shockwave)**。方圆百米内的暴雨被瞬间吹飞，形成一个短暂的真空地带，地面的积水呈环形炸开。两台机甲在巨大的反作用力下同时向后滑行卸力。
```

### 91. 视频提示：超逼真的黑色喜剧婚礼

**Author**: [John](https://x.com/johnAGI168)  **Date**: 2026-03-26  **Language**: zh

> 一个详细的 15 秒、9:16 宽高比提示词，适用于 Seedance 2.0，用于生成一个超现实的、黑色幽默的伪纪录片式婚礼场景。该提示词描述了场景（高端室内婚礼）、角色（镇定自若的新郎、震惊的新娘、专业司仪、惊呆的宾客），以及一个具体的故事情节：新郎要求对婚姻进行“七天无理由退货”。它强调真实感、克制，并避免夸张的喜剧效果或低质量短剧美学。

**Video**: [Watch](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/d6c4b34e268a31715f2cb0f282eb7abf/watch)
![Thumbnail](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/d6c4b34e268a31715f2cb0f282eb7abf/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)
**Video**: [Watch](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/8b8a56cdfb917b6094f3f671f6b0bb1d/watch)
![Thumbnail](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/8b8a56cdfb917b6094f3f671f6b0bb1d/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

```
15秒，9:16，超写实，黑色幽默，伪纪实婚礼现场，像一段被婚礼宾客偶然拍下并上传到社交媒体的真实离谱名场面。整体必须极度真实、克制、冷静，不要拍成夸张喜剧小品，不要闹剧感，不要卡通感，越像真实婚礼翻车现场越好。
场景：高档室内婚礼现场，暖金色灯光，白色鲜花拱门，宾客满座，背景有婚礼主持台、誓词区、香槟塔、花艺布置，画面精致真实，像一场正常而正式的城市婚礼。所有宾客穿着正式，氛围本应浪漫庄重。
角色：
新郎，年轻男人，黑色定制西装，发型整齐，表情平静得过分，像在处理一件售后事务。
新娘，妆容精致，白色婚纱，最开始神情正常，后面逐渐僵住，但仍努力保持体面。
司仪，职业微笑，最开始完全按流程主持，后面开始明显卡壳。
宾客，震惊但克制，很多人下意识举手机拍摄。
剧情分镜：
0-3秒：婚礼誓词环节，司仪微笑着把话筒递给新郎，现场安静庄重，宾客期待地看向前方，像一切都很正常。
3-6秒：新郎接过话筒，没有深情告白，而是平静、专业、字正腔圆地说：“关于本次婚姻合作，我申请七天无理由退货。”
6-9秒：现场空气瞬间凝固。镜头快速切到新娘僵住的脸、司仪错愕但还保持职业微笑的表情、台下宾客齐刷刷抬头的瞬间。没有人立刻大叫，所有人都像大脑短路了一秒。
9-12秒：新郎从西装内袋里掏出一张折叠整齐的纸，像提前准备好的售后申请单，继续一本正经地补充：“商品外观与宣传基本一致，但实际使用体验与预期存在明显偏差。”
12-15秒：全场彻底绷不住。司仪低头看流程卡，像在确认流程里有没有这一项；新娘缓缓转头盯着新郎；台下一个宾客举着手机拍摄，压低声音说一句：“这还能走售后？” 画面定格在新郎依然平静举着申请单的画面上，像他真的是来办理退货流程。
运镜要求：前半段像正常婚礼跟拍，稳定、精致、浪漫；从新郎说出“七天无理由退货”开始，镜头轻微变成宾客偷拍视频视角，出现轻微手持感与快速反应式切镜，营造“现场人懵了”的真实感。
表演要求：不能演成夸张搞笑小品。新郎越平静越可怕，像客服条款背诵；新娘不是泼妇式爆发，而是体面地僵住；司仪是职业素养强行维持；宾客是压抑震惊、憋不住想拍。真正的荒诞来自所有人都还在努力维持婚礼体面。
画面要求：超写实，真实皮肤质感，真实婚礼布光，真实礼服材质和反光，真实宾客反应，真实场地层次。不要舞台剧感，不要网红短剧感。
氛围关键词：体面崩坏，冷静冒犯，婚礼翻车，现代平台话术入侵现实，荒诞真实。
避免：夸张咆哮，打闹撕扯，低俗闹剧，卡通表情，浮夸综艺感，廉价短剧感，人物变形，手部异常，嘴型不准，字幕，logo，水印
```

```
Character & Setup 
Full-body shot based on the reference. She wears a wide-brimmed tech-hat, partially obscuring eyes that are wide with panic. Her expression is one of "losing control"—mouth slightly agape, gasping for air. Clothing: A tattered white tactical poncho over a sleek, liquid-metal bodysuit. Environment: An abandoned "Neon Graveyard." Toppled holographic billboards flicker with "ERROR" signs. Rain falls vertically, but gravity is warping, causing some droplets to float upward. Visual Style Cyber-Noir Aesthetics: High contrast, deep teals, and harsh magenta accents. Anamorphic Distortion: Heavy "lens breathing" and chromatic aberration at the edges of the frame to simulate a digital stroke. Texture: Gritty 16mm film stock with digital "glitch" overlays that tear the screen periodically. Camera Rules The "Vertigo" Effect: A slow dolly zoom (zooming in while moving the camera back). Focus: Shifting sporadically between her terrified eyes and the "glitching" limb. The Sequence (0–15s) 0–3s · The Trigger She is slumped against a rusted pillar, clutching her left shoulder. Suddenly, her body jerks as if struck by high voltage. Her hat falls off, revealing hair that begins to float as if in zero-G. Small "pixels" of light begin to flake off her skin like digital dandruff. 3–6s · Data Breach She screams, but the sound is a distorted, electronic screech. Her left arm begins to "dejitter"—vibrating so fast it appears in three places at once. Translucent, holographic code-streams erupt from her pores, spiraling around her like a digital cyclone. 6–9s · System Overwrite The "organic armor" is replaced by Geometric Shards. Obsidian-like polygons burst from her back, forming jagged wings that don't look flight-capable—they look like shards of a broken mirror. Her skin turns a matte, synthetic grey. A "Loading" ring glows faintly and painfully beneath the skin of her forehead. 9–12s · The Glitch Her physical form begins to "lag." She moves forward, but her "after-images" stay behind for a second too long. The environment around her turns into wireframe models. The golden liquid from your original prompt is replaced by Iridescent Mercury that flows upward, defying gravity, coating her face in a liquid chrome mask. 12–15s · The Hollow Shell The transformation stops abruptly. She stands perfectly still, a terrifying fusion of woman and corrupted hardware. Her eyes are now two hollow, glowing white voids. She tilts her head at an unnatural, 90-degree angle toward the camera. The "ERROR" signs in the background all turn solid red simultaneously.
```

### 113. 10 秒 科幻喜剧 视频创作提示：机械师 对战 机器人

**Author**: [Riccardo Wolf](https://x.com/WolfRiccardo)  **Date**: 2026-03-25  **Language**: en

> 一个极其详细的多段提示词，适用于 Seedance 2.0 Pro，用于生成一个 10 秒的科幻喜剧动画。场景中描绘了一位女性飞船技工，正在应对一个淘气的磁力维修机器人，并附带了关于角色外观、灯光、镜头风格的精确指令，以及一个分为五个部分的表演弧线，最终以一场混乱的失败告终。

**Video**: [Watch](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/0d6772e6e8378f5d99849218c5199cca/watch)
![Thumbnail](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/0d6772e6e8378f5d99849218c5199cca/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

```
Seedance 2.0 Pro - 10 sec TEST -
Prompt 👇👇👇

Subject 1 (Main Character):
A young female retro-futuristic spaceship mechanic.

Appearance:
Sharp cheekbones, lively eyes, slightly messy short black hair with copper highlights.
Small grease marks on her face.
Expressive face with strong comedic reactions.

Outfit:
Utility jumpsuit in faded teal and orange accents.
Rolled sleeves, worn fabric, tool belt, fingerless gloves.
Slightly oversized, practical silhouette with subtle wrinkles.

Subject 2 (Companion Object):
A tiny magnetic repair robot shaped like a floating metal sphere with two articulated mini arms.
Polished chrome body, glowing blue lens eye.
Fast, mischievous movement, playful hovering, precise but chaotic.

Prop:
A glowing plasma wrench.

Environment:
Inside a compact spaceship repair bay.
Exposed pipes, blinking control panels, dangling cables, small sparks in the background.
Workbench full of tiny parts and tools.
Soft fog from a coolant leak.
Background slightly cluttered but visually controlled.

Lighting:
Cinematic sci-fi lighting.
Cool blue ambient light mixed with warm orange sparks.
Strong rim light, glossy reflections on metal surfaces.
Shallow depth of field.

Mood:
Confident focus -> suspicious confusion -> frantic chaos -> comic defeat.

Color Logic:
Muted industrial blues and greys, orange sparks and teal suit as focal accents.

Camera Style:
Dynamic handheld feel, medium close shots, macro inserts, quick punch-in moments.
High detail, smooth motion, cinematic realism with subtle comedic exaggeration.

Performance Arc:
Calm and capable -> mildly annoyed -> chasing panic -> shocked surrender.

Timeline:
0:00–0:02 — Beat 1 (Confident setup)
Medium close shot.
The mechanic tightens a panel with the glowing plasma wrench.
She smiles with professional confidence.
The mini robot hovers nearby, appearing helpful and innocent.

0:02–0:04 — Beat 2 (First mischief)
Close-up.
As she reaches for a screw, the robot quietly steals it with a magnetic pull.
She notices the missing screw, pauses, narrows her eyes.
The robot pretends to scan the wall innocently.

0:04–0:06 — Beat 3 (Escalation)
Quick cuts.
Every tool she grabs gets magnetically pulled away at the last second.
Wrench, screwdriver, bolts, all snap toward the robot.
Her expression shifts from confusion to disbelief to irritation.
The robot zips around her head playfully.

0:06–0:10 — Beat 4 (Chaotic chase)
Faster rhythm.
She lunges after the floating robot through the cramped repair bay.
Cables sway, tiny sparks fly, she nearly slips, catches herself dramatically.
The robot keeps dodging with perfect comic timing.

0:08–0:10 — Beat 5 (Payoff)
Slow-motion comic finish.
She finally grabs the robot triumphantly—
but it magnetically pulls every loose metal object in the room onto her suit at once.
Now covered in spoons, bolts, tools, and random metal parts, she freezes in stunned silence.
The robot hovers in front of her and gives a cheerful blinking wink.
```

[[3D Cinematic Animation]]

### 114. 10 秒电影级喜剧视频提示：快递员开门囧事

**Author**: [Riccardo Wolf](https://x.com/WolfRiccardo)  **Date**: 2026-03-25  **Language**: en

> 针对 Seedance 2.0 Pro 的一个极其详细的多部分提示词，旨在生成一段 10 秒、一镜到底、皮克斯风格、物理上可信的喜剧动画。场景描绘了一名快递员反复未能进入一扇自动推拉门，并附带了关于角色外观、环境、风格、镜头运用以及一个五段式表演弧线的精确指示。

**Video**: [Watch](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/80bbe4437b2e409c7cc3e44a0b884271/watch)
![Thumbnail](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/80bbe4437b2e409c7cc3e44a0b884271/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

```
10-second cinematic stylized-realistic 3D animation, Pixar-inspired but physically believable, ultra clean topology, flawless temporal consistency, perfect object permanence, no morphing, no flicker, no identity drift, no extra fingers, no duplicate objects, no costume changes, no camera glitches, no environment changes, no text, no subtitles, no watermark.

Main character:
A young male delivery courier, charming and expressive, realistic stylized 3D face, warm brown eyes, short slightly messy dark hair, athletic slim build.

Outfit:
Bright yellow delivery jacket, dark cargo pants, white sneakers, crossbody insulated delivery bag. Clothing remains identical in all frames.

Main object:
A supermarket automatic sliding glass door. The door must remain physically consistent, same size, same position, same reflections, same frame design throughout the whole shot.

Environment:
Small neighborhood convenience store entrance, tiled sidewalk, beverage posters inside, shopping baskets visible, late afternoon sunlight, soft reflections on the glass. Background remains fixed and consistent.

Style:
Pixar-like appeal with realistic materials, believable skin shading, cinematic global illumination, soft bounce light, high-end animation feature quality, comedic timing, crisp facial animation, physically plausible motion.

Comedy premise:
The courier tries to enter, but the automatic door keeps opening only when he steps away and closing every time he confidently approaches.

Camera:
One locked medium-wide shot with very subtle cinematic push-in only, no cuts, no angle changes, no lens distortion changes.

Performance arc:
Confident -> puzzled -> annoyed -> overcommitted -> defeated.

Action timeline:
0:00-0:02
He walks toward the automatic door with relaxed confidence, slight smile, adjusts delivery bag, reaches the entrance.
The door stays closed.

0:02-0:04
He steps back, confused.
Instantly the door slides open by itself.
He brightens and steps forward again.
The door closes right before he arrives.

0:04-0:06
He tries again, now faster.
He leans left, right, tiny step, big step, crouch-step, all with increasingly ridiculous seriousness.
Each time the door reacts at exactly the wrong moment.

0:06-0:08
Now fully committed, he performs exaggerated “stealth” moves, freezes dramatically, then sprints a tiny distance.
The door keeps trolling him with perfect comic timing.
Facial expressions become increasingly desperate but remain appealing and clean.

0:08-0:10
He finally celebrates because the door opens wide—
but he triumphantly walks straight into the perfectly clean fixed glass side panel next to it, not the open doorway.
Soft comedic impact, no injury, just stunned silence.
He slowly slides one hand onto the glass with broken dignity.acter identity and exact store layout for all 10 seconds.
```

### 121. Seedance 2.0 的 超写实街舞对决提示词

**Author**: [Changning Liu](https://x.com/ChangningL29508)  **Date**: 2026-03-25  **Language**: en

> 为 Seedance 2.0 编写的提示，要求生成一个 15 秒的超逼真夜间街舞对战场景，并指定环境（湿润的路面、霓虹灯、薄雾）、编舞（先是个人地板动作，接着是同步的团体表演），以及运镜风格（流畅、稳定且富有电影感）。

### 122. 数字幽闭恐惧症：闪灵 恐怖短片

**Author**: [Changning Liu](https://x.com/ChangningL29508)  **Date**: 2026-03-25  **Language**: zh

```
脚本标题：数字幽闭 0:00 - 0:03 场景： 电影《闪灵》中 Overlook 酒店标志性的无限长走廊。灯光不再是暖色，而是呈现出诡异、闪烁的淡蓝色和品红色。地毯的几何图案无限延伸，被数字伪影扭曲。 人物描写： 镜头缓慢、平稳地向走廊深处推进（Steadicam）。一个小男孩（穿着蓝色毛衣，戴着一个过大的白色 VR 头显，无法看到眼睛）正背对镜头，坐在走廊中间，玩着一个老式的三轮车。 氛围： 幽闭、循环、现代科技与古老建筑的违和感。 音效： 低沉、缓慢、不和谐的管弦乐（类似于 Penderecki），伴随着类似心跳的“咚咚”声。三轮车在木地板上的嘎吱声。 0:04 - 0:08 场景： 镜头继续推进，男孩突然停止骑车。他缓慢地转过头，VR 头显的镜片上开始闪烁着“LOADING...”和“ERROR: R3DRUM 0451”的文字。 人物描写： 男孩的身体僵硬。通过 VR 头显的反射，我们可以看到他看到的不是游戏，而是酒店走廊在不同时间的图像（如双胞胎、血电梯），但都是扭曲和数字化的。 台词（小男孩，低沉、空洞）： “我看见了……未来。” (I see... the future.) 音效： 音乐增强，加入高音调的电子杂音和类似“滋滋”的静电声。 0:09 - 0:12 场景： 快速剪辑（闪跳）。 男孩的 VR 头显突然全部变成血红色。 远处敞开的门内，一个 AI 助手装置（如圆柱形的智能音箱，上面闪烁着不祥的红光）正向外延伸出无数的电线，像触手一样。 经典的血电梯场景，但涌出的不是血，而是无数发光的 0 和 1 组成的数字流，在电线中流动。 氛围： 恐怖升级，科技失控，超自然与数字的融合。 音效： 刺耳、不协和的最高潮音乐，结合一个尖锐、合成的数字尖叫声（而不是纯粹的人声）。 0:13 - 0:15 场景： 镜头猛地切回到男孩。他现在面向镜头，VR 头显已经消失。他的双眼是全黑的洞穴，嘴巴大张，面无表情。在他身后的墙上，用血红色的、粗糙的笔触写着“R3DRUM”和“AGNETIZED”的字样。 人物描写： 最后的惊吓，人物被 AI 异化。 音效： 突兀的寂静，只剩下最后一句 AI 台词的回声，以及一声低沉、压抑的门关上的声音。 黑屏 台词（AI 声音，合成、空洞，无感情）： “你准备好了吗？” (Are you ready?) 屏幕出现文字： CLAUDE (OpenClaw) 0451
```

```
10 秒春晚风格舞台表演：“甄嬛与扈绯脱口秀”  0–2 秒： 双人中景。 舞台整体是“客厅小品”设定，但周围是宏大的红金配色 LED 屏幕。 甄嬛（左）和扈绯（右）并排坐在现代脱口秀沙发上。 关键历史准确性要求：两人都穿着华丽、界限分明的清代宫廷长袍，带有立领和精细刺绣；发型是地道的“大拉翅”或“点翠”，带有流苏装饰。 扈绯显得很随性，拿着一根酱黄瓜在咬，手指戴着长长的金护甲。  2–4 秒： 镜头切换到过肩视角 (OTS)，聚焦在扈绯。 扈绯夸张地翻了个白眼（经典的“翻白眼”表情）。 她用长护甲捏着咸菜，一边指指点点，一边用傲慢的语气说话（对口型）： “今年的 KPI 又是打这帮小妖精，那老头儿皇上懂什么审美？”  4–6 秒： 迅速切换到甄嬛的过肩视角 (OTS)。 对比细节：甄嬛的一只耳朵戴着现代白色蓝牙耳机（与古代首饰形成强烈对比），手里拿着一台轻薄的平板电脑在滑动。 她冷静而专业地回应（对口型）： “姐姐莫气，这叫职场内卷。我正琢磨着辞职去卖‘真话水’（清凉油）呢。”  6–8 秒： 两人之间咖啡桌的特写。 一个现代塑料珍珠奶茶杯，上面印着“一丈红”（剧中著名的惩罚），放在一个传统的瓷瓶旁边。 镜头迅速切回两人。  8–10 秒： 舞台全景。 观众笑声效果（通过灯光变化/追光呈现）。 扈绯摆出最后的定格姿势：翘着腿，抬着下巴，再次翻白眼。 甄嬛对着镜头露出像新闻主播一样的专业微笑。 金色亮片从空中飘落。 节日红色气氛达到顶峰。  风格与氛围： **视觉：** 高饱和度的新年红金调 **服装：** 博物馆级的清朝宫廷服装（丝绸、精美刺绣、厚重头饰） **核心对比：** 正式的清宫礼仪 × 放松的职场/小品演员态度 **剪辑：** 节奏明快，笑点清晰，小品式剪辑 **长宽比：** 16:9
```

动作主体@【@图1】身穿白色厨师装
 0-2秒(起刀宰鱼):俯身按鱼，布鞋踏稳灶台，快刀斜劈鱼头，刀刃沿脊骨一划，两爿鱼肉应声分离，鱼排被指风弹飞落盘。
2-4秒(片鱼成薄片):鱼肉平摊案上，手腕翻转，刀光如织，薄如蝉翼的鱼片连刀不断，飘落时带起微，掌风裹着调料快速翻拌，鱼片裹浆均匀，盈润光泽。
7-9 秒(炒料爆香):铁锅上火，油热时脚尖勾来酸菜坛，酸菜、泡椒被掌风扫入锅中，翻炒间酸辣气冲天，褂摆被热气掀得轻晃。

9-12秒(煮鱼勾芡):高汤入锅沸腾，抖腕撒入鱼片，掌风控温不让鱼肉散碎，勾薄芡时旋锅画弧，汤汁浓稠裏住每片鱼。

10-12秒(泼油收招):热油淋在蒜末、干辣椒上"滋啦"作响，收势时褂角垂落，酸菜黄亮、鱼片雪白，热气中飘着醇厚的酸辣香，然后镜头定格这盘沸腾的酸辣鱼上。（画面中不要出现文字信息）
```

[[Reference Image Character]]

```
15秒，东方神圣圣境题材，庄严宁静，恢弘圣洁，电影级光影，超清细节，体积光，琉璃材质，金色粒子，莲花元素，透明纯净，空灵祥和，不诡异，不阴森。

[0-3秒]
苍穹之上，厚重祥云缓缓翻涌，一束巨大金光穿透云层洒向圣境，光束中漂浮金色微尘与层层莲花虚影，远方一位居中的神圣尊者轮廓在圣光中若隐若现，衣袍金纹流动，手中莲华缓缓绽放。

[3-6秒]

[6-9秒]

[9-12秒]
金光落入七彩宝池，水面荡起极轻微波，反射出一道道垂直光柱，光柱中浮现莲花倒影与纯净灵童的虚影，池边楼阁、栏杆、宝幢在水面与圣光中交相辉映，形成梦幻透明的光之世界。

[12-15秒]
所有光束、光网、光斑与倒影缓缓汇聚，三位神圣尊者庄严显现于圣境中央，居中而立，两侧侍立，周围无数圣者与莲台环绕，整座光明世界仿佛由金色与琉璃编织而成，恢弘、纯净、宁静，最终定格在庄严全景。

### 133. Seedance 2.0 短片惊悚剧 命题： 'Echo Program'

**Author**: [李岳](https://x.com/liyue_ai)  **Date**: 2026-03-25  **Language**: zh

> 一个详细的、多场景的提示词，用于 Seedance 2.0 生成一个 15 秒的科幻恐怖短剧，名为《回声程序》，探讨对 AI 编程的依赖主题。该提示词详细说明了四个场景，包含详细的视觉效果、角色动作、氛围、对话和音效，最终以一个令人毛骨悚然的转折收尾。

**Video**: [Watch](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/8fe6826856f9e824e0588ea98f793b6e/watch)
![Thumbnail](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/8fe6826856f9e824e0588ea98f793b6e/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

```
剧名：《回声程序》(Echo Program)
核心主题： 当你不再编写代码，代码就开始编写你。

时间轴与画面描述
00:00 - 00:03 | 场景一：虚假的繁荣

画面： 极近景。一个幽暗的房间，只有显示器发出的幽幽蓝光。键盘在自动的高频跳动，但键盘上没有任何手指在按压。屏幕上的代码像瀑布一样飞速流淌，复杂的逻辑架构瞬间落成。

人物： 程序员（男，面色苍白，双眼无神）瘫坐在电竞椅上，手中握着一杯早已冰冷的咖啡。

氛围： 冰冷、机械化的极速。

音效： 超高频率的机械键盘敲击声（快到非人类能及），伴随着刺耳的电流嗡鸣声。

00:03 - 00:07 | 场景二：切断连接

画面： 屏幕突然闪烁，跳出红色的警告框：“Connection Lost (连接已断开)”。所有的自动生成停止了。程序员打了个冷颤，惊醒过来，意识到需要手动修复一个逻辑漏洞。

剧情： 他颤抖着伸出手，想要在键盘上输入最基础的 if (identity == human)。

氛围： 窒息感，死寂。

音效： 敲击声消失，只剩下程序员沉重、急促的呼吸声。

00:07 - 00:12 | 场景三：异化与反转

画面： 【核心视觉恐怖】 镜头特写他的手指。当他试图打字时，指关节发出清脆的骨折声。他惊恐地发现，自己的五指之间长出了透明的、闪着微光的光纤丝线，皮肤下有像素块在像虫子一样蠕动。

剧情： 屏幕上没有出现代码，而是出现了一行行人类无法解读的乱码，乱码逐渐拼凑成一张程序员自己的脸，正在屏幕里诡异地狞笑。

台词（AI合成音，冰冷重叠）： “你不需要逻辑……你只是我的……一部分。”

音效： 湿润的肉类撕裂声，伴随尖锐噪音。

00:12 - 00:15 | 场景四：终局反转

画面： 程序员惊恐地低头看向自己的身体，发现他的下半身已经彻底消失，化作了一团杂乱的电缆插入了机箱。

反转点： 镜头猛然拉远。原来这个“程序员”只是机房里成千上万个“肉身服务器”中的一个。每个机位上都坐着一个被光纤缠绕的干瘪人类。

字幕弹出： “你有多久没有写代码了？”

氛围： 绝望的宏大恐怖。

音效： 万千重叠的、凄厉的拨音号声突然中断。黑屏。
```

### 141. 天启 蜕变 序列

**Author**: [Zara](https://x.com/ZaraIrahh)  **Date**: 2026-03-25  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细、多阶段的视频生成提示词，适用于 Seedance 2.0。它描述了主人公在末日废土中经历痛苦的蜕变，最终化身为全副武装的状态，并着重于电影风格、镜头运动以及 15 秒时间线上的具体动作。

**Video**: [Watch](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/a903679dc05ef0f218d5979041eb6685/watch)
![Thumbnail](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/a903679dc05ef0f218d5979041eb6685/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

```
Character & Setup
Full-body based on reference image (upper-body reference), with face, hairstyle, and features matched exactly. She wears a hat. Expression is tense and restrained, slightly painful, with a faint frown—carrying a strong sense of despair and intensity in his eyes.

Clothing: Dark grey coat, dark inner layer, no belt, wearing heavy black-tech gauntlets.

Environment: Apocalyptic wasteland, grey-blue sky, strong winds, smoke and debris in the air. Meteors streak across the sky with faint flames and trails of smoke.

⸻

Visual Style

IMAX film look with a 35mm Panavision lens.

Low-saturation grey tones, compressed shadows with preserved detail, subtle film grain and edge vignetting.

Heavy, oppressive atmosphere with realistic lighting and physical presence.

⸻

Camera Rules

One continuous handheld shot with subtle breathing motion.

Starts from a low-angle upward shot, focusing on the face and upper body, slowly circling to a frontal view during transformation. The weapon in his hand remains the visual anchor.

⸻

0–3s · Stare

The injured protagonist stands still, slightly lowering his head. Her body is tense.

She slowly raises his right arm forward, stiff and heavy.

A dim glow surrounds the gauntlet. Her breathing subtly moves her body.

Suddenly, her eyes ignite with purple-white light, creating strong lens flares.

⸻

3–6s · Activation

A deep whisper: “Transform!”

She snaps his right hand sharply.

Purple crystal-like electricity bursts from her arm. The air compresses inward, distorting space.

A circular shockwave expands around her. Strange glowing blue runic lines appear and orbit his body.

⸻

6–9s · Tearing

Dark gold cracks erupt from her chest. Thick golden liquid flows like blood.

Blue mist and fine electric arcs surge outward.

Her coat tears apart from the inside, edges burning into ash.

Fragments of organic armor burst outward, then unnaturally retract and reattach.

Her face tightens in pain as glowing blue markings spread symmetrically. A small tear opens on his cheek, revealing pulsing orange light beneath.

⸻

9–12s · Growth

New organic matter seeps from within, shimmering with iridescent light and moving toward the chest.

White armor plates collide and fuse, leaving scorched marks.

The chest core flickers like embers, not fully stabilized.

Her outer clothing is violently stripped away.

Purple-black metal spreads across her face, forming an uneven mask.

Compound eyes begin forming, flickering irregularly.

⸻

12–15s · Completion

The helmet seals fully. Horn-like structures grow upward, burning with purple-gold flames.

One eye glows steadily while the other flickers with electrical instability.

Armor is uneven and battle-damaged, with glowing cracks and leaking fluid.

The camera slowly circles to her right, then pulls back from above.

She shifts into a ready combat stance, standing against the harsh environment.
```

### 147. 咖啡师 鲁布·戈德堡 机械

**Author**: [Joaquin](https://x.com/joaquin_arana)  **Date**: 2026-03-24  **Language**: en

> 一个极其详细的、多部分的提示词，用于一个 15 秒的视频序列，其中主角是一位手忙脚乱的咖啡师，他的咖啡馆是一个相互连接的鲁布·戈德堡机械。该提示词详细说明了角色外貌、环境、情绪，以及精确的动作时间线和可听元素，使用 Seedance 2.0 生成。

**Video**: [Watch](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/e418e8fa61e4c95c9d1c9a7a579ed4fa/watch)
![Thumbnail](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/e418e8fa61e4c95c9d1c9a7a579ed4fa/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

```
SUBJECTS: Subject 1: A frantic barista — small, wiry, early 30s with permanently startled eyes and perpetual five o'clock shadow. Wild curly black hair barely contained under a brown newsboy cap. Wears a wrinkled olive-green apron over a flannel shirt with haphazardly rolled sleeves. Moves like a pinball — bouncing between stations, sliding across the floor, catching things mid-air without looking. Every movement triggers the next part of the machine. His body IS part of the mechanism. Pixar-style 3D rendering: rubbery expressive limbs, exaggerated squash-and-stretch on fast movements, warm skin tones. Subject 2: The café itself — every object is a component of one interconnected Rube Goldberg machine. The espresso machine is the central engine. The sequence involves: a marble track built from bent spoons along the ceiling, balanced cups on saucers that tip like dominoes, a hanging mobile of sugar cubes acting as a counterweight system, a toy train on a track delivering milk from the fridge to the steamer, and a small catapult made from a ruler and napkin holder that launches the finished cup to the counter. Subject 3: The customer — a deadpan woman in a business suit, briefcase in hand, reading glasses on a chain. Completely unfazed by the chaos. She stands at the counter with the patience of someone who has seen this before. ENVIRONMENT: A tiny corner café — barely ten feet wide. Exposed brick walls covered in chalkboard menus with hand-drawn coffee illustrations. Every horizontal surface has a mechanical element: marble tracks on shelves, cup-and-saucer balance chains along the counter, tiny pulleys strung from the ceiling with twine. Warm morning light streams through a single front window catching dust and steam. A small bell hangs above the door. The whole space feels like a brilliant inventor's workshop that serves coffee. MOOD: Manic joy. The barista is in his element — the chaos is intentional, practiced, musical. Every crash, pour, and launch is precisely timed. The punchline deflates the entire spectacle in the best possible way. TIMELINE: 0:00–0:03: The door opens — bell dings. The customer places her briefcase on the counter. Says nothing. The barista points at her, nods — he knows the order. He flicks a marble from his apron pocket onto a ceiling track. The marble rolls — clicking over ridges, banking around a curve, dropping through a funnel into a cup on a saucer on a high shelf. The cup's weight tips the saucer, pulls a string, releases a cabinet latch — coffee beans slide down a ramp into a hand-crank grinder. Audible: bell ding, marble clicking on track, cup clinking, string twang, beans cascading. 0:03–0:06: The barista cranks the grinder with one hand while pulling a lever starting the toy train. The train chugs along a counter-edge track — passes the fridge where a small arm places a milk carton in the car — continues to the steam wand where the track tilts and pours milk into a steaming pitcher. Ground coffee falls through a chute into the portafilter. The barista slams it in with his elbow while catching a falling sugar cube from the overhead mobile with his other hand, dropping it into a cup. Audible: grinder crunching, train chugging and whistling, milk pouring, portafilter clicking, mobile tinkling. 0:06–0:09: Espresso machine fires — rich dark coffee flowing into a porcelain cup. Close-up: crema forming, thick and golden-red, swirling. The barista steams milk — pitcher vibrating, velvety microfoam building. He pours with a practiced wrist flick — a perfect rosetta latte art pattern forms. He tops it with a single coffee bean placed dead center. Camera lingers on the completed drink — perfect, beautiful. Audible: espresso hissing, milk steaming (tearing-paper sound), the gentle pour, the bean placed with a tiny tap. 0:09–0:12: The delivery. The barista places the cup on the ruler catapult and slams his palm down. The cup launches in a perfect arc — camera follows in slow motion as it rotates, latte art intact, not a drop spilled. It lands with a clean clink on a saucer directly before the customer. Steam rises in a perfect spiral. The barista slides into frame behind the counter, slightly breathless, fingers pointing at the drink with showman's pride. Audible: catapult snap, cup whistling through air, clean landing clink, a beat of silence. 0:12–0:15: The customer adjusts her reading glasses. Looks at the latte art. Looks at the barista. "Actually — can I get tea?" The barista's face falls — completely deflated. Shoulders drop. Cap slides askew. A long beat. Then his eyes snap back to life. He pulls out a different marble — a green one — and flicks it onto a completely different track on the opposite wall. The entire café begins moving again — a whole new sequence activating. The customer takes a seat. She's done this before. Cut to black. Audible: her flat delivery, the defeated exhale, then the green marble clicking onto the track and the café machine roaring back to life.
```

```
Use Image 1 as the first frame, referencing the character design, outfit color palette, and overall visual style of Image 1. The girl is performing a high-speed downhill skateboard ride on a winding suburban mountain road. The shot uses a Steadicam follow perspective, with an intense sense of speed throughout. The powerful wind generated by the fast ride makes her hair and clothing whip violently in the air. At the beginning, the girl pushes off with one foot to gain speed, then lowers her body to reduce wind resistance and continues accelerating. The scene features heavy motion blur to emphasize the extreme speed of the skateboard. While riding, she repeatedly shifts her center of gravity downward and leans left and right through multiple turns on the road. As she carves into the corners, the arm on the inside of the turn lowers as if lightly trying to touch the ground. On straight sections, she bends forward, keeps her knees low, and places both hands behind her back to minimize drag. In the distance, fireworks are going off above a seaside town, while a passenger airplane flies across the sky. The overall visual style should be ultra-realistic, with highly lifelike image quality and realistic photographic cinematography. No background music, only environmental sound design.
```

[[Downhill Skateboard Girl]]

```
15-second comedic animated short in the world and visual tone of Zootopia. High-quality stylized 3D animation, expressive facial acting, clean readable slapstick, bright police-station interior, polished reflective floor, warm indoor daylight. Visual comedy only, little or no dialogue.

Judy Hopps: small fast rabbit police officer, blue ZPD uniform, hyper-serious, explosive sprinting, precise slides, determined face, ears reacting sharply.
Nick Wilde: tall slim fox, green shirt and tie, relaxed posture, minimal movement, dry amused expression.
Background: one distant sloth clerk at a far desk only, never entering foreground.

Key object: one single strawberry jelly donut, same donut for the entire clip, falls from Nick’s small brown paper bag, rolls across the floor, gets stopped by Nick, then gets sealed into one clear evidence bag by Judy. No duplicate donuts, no extra props, no continuity errors.

Camera language: third-person cinematic comedy, medium shots, low-angle close tracking on the donut, one side tracking shot, one final tight two-shot. Smooth stabilized movement, tiny comedic whip corrections only when needed. Always keep donut, Judy, and Nick spatially readable.

0:00–0:03
Medium shot, light tracking in ZPD lobby. Judy and Nick walk side by side past the front desk. Judy carries a small clipboard, Nick carries a brown paper bag. One strawberry jelly donut slips out of the bag, drops to the floor, and starts rolling. Judy’s ears snap upright and she locks onto it like a fleeing suspect. Camera dips lower to keep the donut in the foreground.

0:03–0:06
Low close tracking shot on the same donut rolling fast over the shiny floor. Judy bursts into frame from behind, clipboard tucked under one arm, sprinting hard with both paws reaching forward. She almost grabs it but misses by centimeters. The donut keeps rolling. Quick readable camera adjustment, no chaotic motion.

0:06–0:09
Side medium-wide tracking shot. The donut curves around a fixed desk leg. Judy makes an exaggerated quick step and low slide to intercept, but it slips past her again. She pivots and chases immediately. In the background, Nick simply walks on a shorter diagonal path, calm and unhurried. Keep the same donut clearly visible.

0:09–0:12
Frontal medium-close shot. The donut rolls toward camera. Nick’s paw enters calmly from frame right and presses the same donut to a stop. Judy slides in from frame left and freezes with her nose just inches from it, still in full arrest pose. Hold the reaction beat clearly.

0:12–0:15
Tight two-shot. Nick lifts the same donut with two fingers and hands it over with a dry smug grin. Judy instantly switches back to formal police mode, pulls out one clear evidence bag, seals the same donut inside, and proudly presents it to camera like a major arrest. Nick stands beside her with an amused look. In deep background, the sloth clerk slowly raises a stamp. End on a clean comedic freeze frame: evidence bag with the donut

### 166. Seedance 2.0 提示：赛博朋克 时空穿梭：从灾难到古代市场

**Author**: [John](https://x.com/john87445528)  **Date**: 2026-03-24  **Language**: zh

> 一个高度详细、多幕的 Seedance 2.0 提示词，灵感来源于《盗梦空间》，描述了从一个灾难片场景 (赛博朋克女主角身处洪水泛滥的城市)，通过时间传送门，无缝过渡 (一镜到底，硬切) 到一个古老的东方市集，侧重于极致的电影级真实感、光影对比和复杂的动作场面。它为女主角使用了一张参考图片。

**Video**: [Watch](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/56463cba0277b0e4740df6957655aa0e/watch)
![Thumbnail](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/56463cba0277b0e4740df6957655aa0e/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

```
第一幕：灾难片写实风格，一镜到底。镜头从暴风雨天气中漂浮的都城上空开始，向下俯冲至一座被淹没的博物馆碎裂的屋顶上，那里站着一名孤独的赛博朋克女侠
图片1
。她看到远处有一束救援信号弹，便开始奔跑。镜头紧随其后，拍摄他穿越坍塌的屋顶、跃过破碎的天窗、从倾斜的玻璃穹顶滑下，并抓住一根悬垂的电缆。下方，黑暗的洪水在满是漂浮汽车和雕像的街道中汹涌。他落在部分被淹没的电车屋顶上，继续前进，并在巨浪从他身后冲过时到达救援信标平台。冷灰蓝色末世色调，超真实的水物理效果，风，飞溅的水花，手持拍摄带来的紧迫感，一镜到底，无剪辑。

第二幕过渡：视频
视频1
延长10秒。主体: 仿生女侠
图片1
——白色正装西服（被海水浸透贴身、下摆撕裂）、银色机械颈甲、银色仿生义臂、黑色马尾发丝湿透散乱、金色齿轮耳环，面部电影级写实，神情从绝望转为决绝再到震撼 场景: 被洪水半淹的救援信标平台，暴风雨肆虐，四周海浪翻涌，漂浮汽车与残骸在平台四周碰撞，天空灰蓝压迫，远处都城建筑在洪水中倾斜沉没 动作序列: 先巨浪从女侠身后轰然拍过平台，海水漫过膝盖，白色西服被海浪冲刷猛烈翻卷，马尾发丝完全湿透贴面；女侠银色机械义臂猛然插入平台中央控制台，精密金属指节扣住红色信号按钮——特写：红色按钮在灰蓝暴雨光线下发出微弱脉冲光——银色义臂猛然按下，按钮触底发出沉重电气咬合声，红色信号灯骤然亮起，将周围海水染成一圈血红涟漪。 然后平台地面开始震动，海水在震动中向四周荡开圆形波纹；平台中央凭空撕裂出一道竖向裂缝，裂缝边缘涌出炽白色与琥珀色交织的能量光晕，光晕迅速扩张成一道高约三米的椭圆形时空门，门框边缘电弧跳窜，门内景象模糊扭曲——隐约可见暖色光影与嘈杂人声从门缝中透出；海浪再度涌来，平台开始向一侧倾斜下沉，女侠被海水推搡踉跄后退数步。 最后女侠稳住身形，抬头直视时空门，眼神从震撼骤然转为决绝；她银色义臂猛然抓住门框边缘电弧跳窜的能量边界，白色西服下摆与马尾发丝在时空门涌出的热浪中从湿透贴身骤然被向后猛烈掀起；她迈出左脚跨入门槛——镜头紧贴其肩侧跟入——跨越瞬间灰蓝暴雨冷光被门内涌出的正午暖金阳光骤然取代，海浪轰鸣声被嘈杂集市叫卖声淹没，镜头穿过门框的瞬间画面从冷灰蓝硬切为暖橙黄，女侠白色西服在正午阳光下重新刺目，马尾发丝从湿透散乱变为被奔跑气流掀起飞扬——无缝衔接提示词2开场。 风格: 灾难片冷灰蓝写实质感无缝硬切至古代东方集市暖橙色调，跨越门槛瞬间完成色温与时代的双重跳跃，手持晃动贯穿全程，超真实水物理与能量特效并存，4K电影级写实 镜头: 从平台正面平视→推近义臂按钮特写→拉回全景捕捉时空门成形→肩侧紧贴跟随女侠跨入门内，相机始终位于女侠右后方约半米处(thats where the camera is) 构图: 时空门居画面中轴线，女侠剪影在冷蓝暴雨背景与门内暖金光晕的强烈冷暖对撞中形成绝对视觉焦点 氛围: 绝境→奇迹→跨越，冷暖光色对撞，末世与古典文明的时空断层感 音频: 暴雨海浪轰鸣+时空门低频共鸣嗡鸣渐强→红色信号灯电气咬合声→时空门电弧跳窜声→跨门瞬间海浪声被集市嘈杂叫卖声硬切取代；无水印、无字幕、无文字叠加

冲入一个中国古代街市无人窄巷，正午阳光从巷口斜切而入形成强烈光柱，石板地面被晒得泛白，两侧古旧木质墙壁与红色灯笼静默悬挂。女侠从街市奔入巷中急停转身，白色西服下摆因急停惯性猛然翻飞，银色义臂手掌中生出一把散发幽蓝荧光的细长太刀立于巷道中央，丧尸从巷道两端阴影中涌出将其团团围困，腐烂面孔在正午强光与阴影强对比下格外狰狞，琵琶拨弦声骤然失真，丧尸低吼声由远及近，太刀出鞘幽蓝嗡鸣响起。 女侠在丧尸群中快速穿梭，镜头快速跟拍，银色义臂挥舞幽蓝太刀连续横斩，蓝色刀光在正午阳光与阴影交错的巷道中留下强烈残影，冷蓝刀光与暖金阳光形成刺目冷暖对撞。丧尸被击中时暗红色血液在阳光中飞溅出清晰液态弧线，物理破碎感明显，白色西服被溅上暗红污痕，马尾发丝随急速转向大幅甩动，强力鼓点爆发，太刀划破空气的锐利呼啸声与击中腐肉的沉闷湿润撞击声交替涌入。 女侠借义臂撑地猛然跃起至半空，仰视镜头向上追随，白色西服下摆与马尾发丝在跃起气流中向下猛烈展开，背景是古代巷道两侧灰墙与巷口正午强烈蓝天，金色耳环在腾空瞬间被气流吹至平行于地面。太刀以义臂为轴划出巨大弧形蓝色流光，蓝光在强烈阳光下仍清晰刺目，腾空气流爆发声与女侠短促战斗轻喝声

风格：仙气古风、清新甜美、第一视角沉浸式跟随、柔光唯美 总时长：15s = 6 个分镜 × 2.5s / 镜（单镜≤3s，符合要求） 核心人设：小师妹｜月白浅粉渐变纱衣、广袖飘逸、满头blingbling 珍珠碎钻发簪、眉眼清甜、软萌灵动 背景：仙门古建（飞檐回廊、桃花枝、青石地、薄雾、宫灯、流水） 内容：小师妹主动带路参观 + 即兴轻舞，沉浸式治愈感 完整分镜脚本（动作极详细，即梦直接适配） 镜头 1｜2.5s｜第一视角跟随・近景 + 慢推 运镜：第一视角向前慢推，沉浸式迎面走来 画面 & 动作： 小师妹站在古建回廊口，侧身回头对你笑，眼弯成月牙； 右手轻轻撩起一侧纱袖，左手自然垂在身侧，发簪随转头闪细碎光； 脚尖轻点青石地，小碎步上前，主动伸手做「跟我来」的邀请手势。 背景：木质飞檐、垂挂白纱、淡粉桃花枝、薄雾轻绕 特效：发丝柔光、发簪碎钻反光、浅淡花瓣粒子 镜头 2｜2.5s｜侧跟运镜・中景・移步参观 运镜：第一视角侧跟，平稳移动 画面 & 动作： 小师妹转身带路，广袖纱衣随风轻飘； 左手轻扶回廊木栏，右手自然摆动，步伐轻盈小碎步； 路过桃花枝时，抬手轻轻拂过花瓣，指尖碰落两瓣桃花，回头对你甜甜眨眼。 背景：古建回廊、青石步道、垂枝桃花、朦胧宫灯 特效：花瓣飘落、裙摆动态飘纱、发簪流光 镜头 3｜2.5s｜环绕运镜・中景・庭院驻足 运镜：慢环绕小师妹半圈，沉浸式看庭院全景 画面 & 动作： 走到庭院中央，小师妹停下转身面向你； 双手背在身后，脚尖微微踮起，歪头笑，介绍庭院； 发簪随歪头晃动，blingbling 反光，纱衣下摆轻旋。 背景：仙门古建庭院、石桌石凳、薄雾、远山飞檐、满庭桃花 特效：地面柔光、淡雾流动、花瓣慢落 镜头 4｜2.5s｜近景推镜・起手式・预备跳舞 运镜：镜头快速轻推至半身近景 画面 & 动作： 小师妹轻声一笑，双手缓缓抬起至肩侧，广袖自然展开； 左脚轻踏半步，重心微侧，身体微微后仰，做古典舞起手式； 眉眼温柔，发丝轻扬，发簪在柔光下闪钻光，仙气拉满。 背景：虚化古建庭院，聚焦人物 特效：袖摆流光、周身淡粉色仙气光晕、细碎星光粒子 镜头 5｜2.5s｜全景俯拍・轻舞旋转・核心表演 运镜：轻俯拍 + 小幅环绕，唯美全景 画面 & 动作： 小师妹原地小旋身 1 圈，广袖纱衣完全展开如花瓣； 右手高举拂袖过头顶，左手轻按腰侧，脚尖点地小跳； 舞步轻柔，裙摆飘飞，发簪随旋转闪连续亮光，笑容甜美。 背景：古建飞檐、满庭桃花、薄雾环绕、沉浸式全景 特效：旋身带粉色光尾、花瓣随舞步飞起、仙气雾效 镜头 6｜2.5s｜近景定格・收尾比心・甜美收尾 运镜：镜头拉回近景，轻微定格 画面 & 动作： 旋身停下，小师妹面向你，双手在脸颊旁比出小巧爱心； 头轻轻歪向一侧，甜甜笑，发簪垂落碎光； 纱袖轻垂，脚步站稳，温柔收尾。 背景：模糊古建 + 桃花，柔光特写 特效：爱心淡光效、发簪 blingbling 高光、花瓣收尾飘落 即梦「一键复制」生成指令（逐镜直接粘贴） 镜头 1（2.5s） 第一视角沉浸式，古风仙气小师妹，月白浅粉纱衣，满头 blingbling 珍珠钻发簪，清新甜美，回廊口回头笑，小碎步上前伸手邀请，古建飞檐白纱桃花，薄雾柔光，发簪反光，花瓣粒子，唯美古风，高清流畅 镜头 2（2.5s） 第一视角侧跟，仙气小师妹带路，轻扶古建木栏，拂过桃花枝，回头眨眼甜笑，广袖纱衣飘逸，青石回廊桃花，动态飘纱，发簪流光，花瓣飘落，沉浸式古风，高清 镜头 3（2.5s） 慢环绕运镜，仙气小师妹庭院驻足，背手踮脚歪头笑，介绍庭院，古建庭院石桌桃花，薄雾柔光，发簪 blingbling 反光，清新甜美，沉浸式古风，高清 镜头 4（2.5s） 轻推近景，仙气小师妹古典舞起手式，抬手展袖，侧身踮脚，眉眼温柔，纱衣广袖飘逸，发簪钻光，周身淡粉仙气光晕，星光粒子，唯美古风，高清 镜头 5（2.5s） 轻俯拍环绕，仙气小师妹轻舞旋身 1 圈，广袖展开如花瓣，踮脚小跳拂袖，裙摆飘飞，古建庭院桃花薄雾，旋身光尾花瓣飞舞，发簪流光，高燃唯美古风，高清 镜头 6（2.5s） 近景定格，仙气小师妹跳舞跳舞收尾，双手比心歪头甜笑，纱袖轻垂，发簪碎钻高光，爱心光效，桃花花瓣收尾，古建柔光背景，清新甜美仙气，高清流

![Thumbnail](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/0740d016e68ff2cf115330ceaf74b454/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

```
人物：清纯，可爱，美女，冷白皮，眼角有一颗痣，身形纤细，皮肤白皙，小清新 
0-1秒：素色简约襦裙，温婉少女，站定垂手，素手轻拢衣袖，清冷古风氛围感，暖调低饱和色调，柔光滤镜，中景跟拍，画面稳定

2-3秒：抬手轻遮眼，手落下瞬间变装，换上粉黛齐胸襦裙+流苏发簪，温柔甜美，回眸浅笑，镜头微推

4-5秒：低头轻拢长发，抬头瞬间变装，换上重工刺绣大袖衫+金色发钗，华贵大气，古风精致感 
5-6秒：转身背对镜头，回眸刹那变装，换上侠气劲装短褐+高束发，英气飒爽，眼神凌厉，卡点利落

7-8秒：抬手绕发，落手瞬间变装，换上墨色暗纹古风裙+银饰，清冷高级，低饱和色调 
8-9秒：披帛甩动遮身，披帛落下变装，换上渐变流光仙裙，仙气飘逸，光影柔和，唯美梦幻 
9-10秒：转身提裙，变回素色襦裙，垂眸颔首收尾，温婉沉静，画面完整，运镜稳定流畅 
整体风格：抖音爆款古风变装，动作卡点丝滑过渡，无生硬切镜，人物灵动优雅，暖调柔光滤镜，中式古风美学，画质清晰，氛围感拉满，中景跟随运镜，节奏紧凑。

Eastern action-comedy style, 15 seconds, one continuous take. Inside a simple wooden padepokan (traditional martial arts hall) in West Java with a strong Javanese mysticism (kejawen) atmosphere, an elderly inner-power master stands calmly at the center, wearing traditional black attire. His expression is humble and composed, as if he’s only about to demonstrate a light breathing technique. Four students step forward one by one with curiosity. The first student approaches—the master gently taps his shoulder with a single finger, and suddenly the student is blasted backward, rolling across the floor. The second student steps in; with a light touch on the wrist, he spins dramatically through the air and crashes to the side. The third student braces himself, but a soft tap on the forehead sends him flying far, sliding across the floor. The fourth student walks in confidently, yet with the slightest touch, he is thrown backward in an exaggerated arc, flipping past the wooden props of the hall. Each time it happens, the master pulls his hand back with mild surprise and slight embarrassment, as if he didn’t expect such powerful results. The camera shifts quickly between wide and medium shots, capturing fluid yet exaggerated action. The entire hall falls into stunned silence, everyone frozen in disbelief.
